srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e0/U.S._Marine_Corps_HC-130_Hercules_aircraft_assigned_to_the_3rd_Marine_Expeditionary_Brigade_and_other_military_aircraft_sit_on_the_tarmac_at_an_airport_in_Guiuan%2C_Philippines%2C_waiting_to_airlift_Philippine_131117-N-XN177-381.jpg/330px-thumbnail.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e0/U.S._Marine_Corps_HC-130_Hercules_aircraft_assigned_to_the_3rd_Marine_Expeditionary_Brigade_and_other_military_aircraft_sit_on_the_tarmac_at_an_airport_in_Guiuan%2C_Philippines%2C_waiting_to_airlift_Philippine_131117-N-XN177-381.jpg/440px-thumbnail.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2331" data-file-height="1551" /></a>\n<div class="thumbcaption">\n<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:U.S._Marine_Corps_HC-130_Hercules_aircraft_assigned_to_the_3rd_Marine_Expeditionary_Brigade_and_other_military_aircraft_sit_on_the_tarmac_at_an_airport_in_Guiuan,_Philippines,_waiting_to_airlift_Philippine_131117-N-XN177-381.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>\nDevastated <a href="/wiki/Coconut" title="Coconut">coconut</a> trees in Guiuan</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n<p>Typhoon Haiyan knocked over Power Barge 103 of <a href="/wiki/National_Power_Corporation" title="National Power Corporation">NAPOCOR</a> in <a href="/wiki/Estancia,_Iloilo" title="Estancia, Iloilo">Estancia, Iloilo</a> causing an oil spill.<sup id="cite_ref-100" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-100">[96]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-101" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-101">[97]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-102" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-102">[98]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-103" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-103">[99]</a></sup> As a result of the typhoon, the government is planning to replant <a href="/wiki/Mangrove" title="Mangrove">mangroves</a> in coastal areas while preserving the remaining ones.<sup id="cite_ref-104" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-104">[100]</a></sup> Affected residents were allowed to return to their homes by the Department of Health on December 7, 2013 after an air quality test found out that <a href="/wiki/Benzene" title="Benzene">benzene</a> levels in affected areas reached near-zero parts per million. Earlier, residents were asked to evacuate affected areas as the benzene levels had reached unhealthy amounts.<sup id="cite_ref-105" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-105">[101]</a></sup></p>\n<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Looting_and_violence">Looting and violence</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Typhoon_Haiyan&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Looting and violence">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>\n<div class="thumb tleft">\n<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Tacloban_Typhoon_Haiyan_2013-11-13.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d0/Tacloban_Typhoon_Haiyan_2013-11-13.jpg/220px-Tacloban_Typhoon_Haiyan_2013-11-13.jpg" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d0/Tacloban_Typhoon_Haiyan_2013-11-13.jpg/330px-Tacloban_Typhoon_Haiyan_2013-11-13.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d0/Tacloban_Typhoon_Haiyan_2013-11-13.jpg/440px-Tacloban_Typhoon_Haiyan_2013-11-13.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4608" data-file-height="3072" /></a>\n<div class="thumbcaption">\n<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Tacloban_Typhoon_Haiyan_2013-11-13.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>\nThe remains of a home destroyed by the storm in Tacloban City.</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n<p>Throughout Tacloban City, widespread <a href="/wiki/Looting" title="Looting">looting</a> took place in the days following Haiyan\'s passage. In some instances, relief trucks were attacked and had food stolen in the city. Two of the city\'s malls and numerous grocery stores were subjected to looting. A fuel depot in the city was guarded by armed police while 200 additional officers were dispatched to assist.<sup id="cite_ref-CBSNov10_106-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CBSNov10-106">[102]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Security_checkpoint" title="Security checkpoint">Security checkpoints</a> had since been set up all over Tacloban and a <a href="/wiki/Curfew" title="Curfew">curfew</a> was imposed on residents to prevent more attacks.<sup id="cite_ref-107" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-107">[103]</a></sup> Philippine military forces also prevented members of the <a href="/wiki/New_People%27s_Army" title="New People\'s Army">New People\'s Army</a> from ambushing a relief convoy bound for Samar in <a href="/wiki/Matnog,_Sorsogon" title="Matnog, Sorsogon">Matnog, Sorsogon</a>, killing two.<sup id="cite_ref-108" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-108">[104]</a></sup> President <a href="/wiki/Benigno_Aquino_III" title="Benigno Aquino III">Benigno Aquino III</a> considered declaring <a href="/wiki/Martial_law" title="Martial law">martial law</a> in hopes of restoring order in affected areas.<sup id="cite_ref-109" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-109">[105]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-harlan_wapo_110-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-harlan_wapo-110">[106]</a></sup></p>\n<p>Looting intensified as slow recovery efforts forced residents to seek any means necessary to survive. Tacloban city administrator Tecson John Lim stated, "The looting is not criminality. It is self-preservation." The <i><a href="/wiki/Chicago_Tribune" title="Chicago Tribune">Chicago Tribune</a></i> reported that some areas were on the brink of anarchy, though <a href="/wiki/Secretary_of_the_Interior_and_Local_Government_(Philippines)" title="Secretary of the Interior and Local Government (Philippines)">Interior Secretary</a> <a href="/wiki/Mar_Roxas" title="Mar Roxas">Mar Roxas</a> denied such claims.<sup id="cite_ref-ChicagoTribuneNov13_57-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ChicagoTribuneNov13-57">[53]</a></sup> Further complicating efforts to retain order was the lack of officers reporting for work. In Tacloban, only 100 of the city\'s 1,300 police personnel reported for duty.<sup id="cite_ref-LATimesNov12_93-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-LATimesNov12-93">[89]</a></sup> In <a href="/wiki/Alangalang,_Leyte" title="Alangalang, Leyte">Alangalang</a>, just west of Tacloban, eight people were crushed to death after the walls of a warehouse collapsed during a raid on a government rice stockpile. Approximately 33,000 bags of rice, each weighing 50&#160;kg (110&#160;lb), were stolen. Warehouses were also raided in <a href="/wiki/Jaro,_Leyte" title="Jaro, Leyte">Jaro</a> and <a href="/wiki/Palo,_Leyte" title="Palo, Leyte">Palo</a>. Throughout the city of Tacloban itself, people began looting from homes as stores had been completely emptied.<sup id="cite_ref-ChicagoTribuneNov13_57-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ChicagoTribuneNov13-57">[53]</a></sup></p>\n<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Criticism_of_government_response">Criticism of government response</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Typhoon_Haiyan&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Criticism of government response">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>\n<div class="thumb tright">\n<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Typhoon_Haiyan_deaths_in_Eastern_Visayas_map.png" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/95/Typhoon_Haiyan_deaths_in_Eastern_Visayas_map.png/220px-Typhoon_Haiyan_deaths_in_Eastern_Visayas_map.png" width="220" height="179" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/9/95/Typhoon_Haiyan_deaths_in_Eastern_Visayas_map.png 1.5x" data-file-width="277" data-file-height="225" /></a>\n<div class="thumbcaption">\n<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Typhoon_Haiyan_deaths_in_Eastern_Visayas_map.png" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>\nColor coded map of Eastern Visayas showing the number of deaths caused by Typhoon Haiyan.<br />\n<span style="margin:0; font-size:90%; white-space:nowrap;"><span class="legend-text" style="border:none; padding:1px .6em; background-color:#6D1014; color:black; font-size:95%; line-height:1.25; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;More than 1,000</span><br />\n<span style="margin:0; font-size:90%; white-space:nowrap;"><span class="legend-text" style="border:none; padding:1px .6em; background-color:#DA1F28; color:black; font-size:95%; line-height:1.25; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;500-999</span><br />\n<span style="margin:0; font-size:90%; white-space:nowrap;"><span class="legend-text" style="border:none; padding:1px .6em; background-color:#F2A4A7; color:black; font-size:95%; line-height:1.25; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;100-499</span><br />\n<span style="margin:0; font-size:90%; white-space:nowrap;"><span class="legend-text" style="border:none; padding:1px .6em; background-color:#C3D69B; color:black; font-size:95%; line-height:1.25; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;50-99</span><br />\n<span style="margin:0; font-size:90%; white-space:nowrap;"><span class="legend-text" style="border:none; padding:1px .6em; background-color:#9BBB59; color:black; font-size:95%; line-height:1.25; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;25-49</span><br />\n<span style="margin:0; font-size:90%; white-space:nowrap;"><span class="legend-text" style="border:none; padding:1px .6em; background-color:#4F6228; color:black; font-size:95%; line-height:1.25; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;1-24</span><br />\n<span style="margin:0; font-size:90%; white-space:nowrap;"><span class="legend-text" style="border:none; padding:1px .6em; background-color:#B9B9B9; color:black; font-size:95%; line-height:1.25; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;0</span></div>\n</div>\n</div>\n<p>Condemnations of slow government action in the relief effort in response to the typhoon mounted days after the storm had passed. Media reports criticized the Aquino administration for apparent lack of preparation and coordination among government agencies in the aid operation.<sup id="cite_ref-111" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-111">[107]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-112" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-112">[108]</a></sup> Up until November 12, five days after the typhoon struck, survivors continued to struggle with basic necessities such as food, water, and shelter while remote towns in <a href="/wiki/Leyte" title="Leyte">Leyte</a> and <a href="/wiki/Samar" title="Samar">Samar</a> were yet to be reached by aid.<sup id="cite_ref-113" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-113">[109]</a></sup> The Philippine government responded by saying that they have dealt with the tragedy "quite well" but the response had been slow due to the breakdown of the local governance in affected areas where officials and employees, who were usually the first to respond in these events, were victims of the typhoon themselves.<sup id="cite_ref-114" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-114">[110]</a></sup> Cabinet Secretary <a href="/wiki/Jose_Rene_Almendras" title="Jose Rene Almendras">Jose Rene Almendras</a> said that the national government had to take over despite logistical challenges and assured it is working toward providing aid the quickest way possible to the survivors.<sup id="cite_ref-115" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-115">[111]</a></sup> The national Government was also criticized for putting the responsibility of handling the dead to the Bureau of Fire instead to the Department of Health. Dr. Racquel Fortun, one of the forensic experts to go to the area three days after the typhoon insisted that handling of the bodies is a health matter and therefore a responsibility of DOH.<sup id="cite_ref-116" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-116">[112]</a></sup></p>\n<p>One of the biggest controversies of Typhoon Haiyan is probably the number of the victims or the body count. According to the Philippine government sources, the number of those killed during the typhoon ranges from 4,000 to 6,000 individuals while some sources claim that the body count reaches up to 15,000.<sup id="cite_ref-117" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-117">[113]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-118" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-118">[114]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-119" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-119">[115]</a></sup></p>\n<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Humanitarian_crisis_and_population_displacement">Humanitarian crisis and population displacement</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Typhoon_Haiyan&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Humanitarian crisis and population displacement">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>\n<p>The Philippines faced a humanitarian crisis days after the typhoon hit much of the <a href="/wiki/Visayas" title="Visayas">Visayas</a> with 1.9 million homeless and more than 6,000,000 displaced.<sup id="cite_ref-120" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-120">[116]</a></sup> In <a href="/wiki/Tacloban" title="Tacloban">Tacloban</a> alone, ninety percent of the structures are either destroyed or damaged while other cities, such as <a href="/wiki/Ormoc" title="Ormoc">Ormoc</a>, are reporting similar damage.<sup id="cite_ref-121" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-121">[117]</a></sup> The United Nations fear that the possibility of the spread of disease is high due to the lack of food, water, shelter, and medication. Casualties have been reported as a result of the lack of aid in affected areas and the number of dead is likely to rise.<sup id="cite_ref-122" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-122">[118]</a></sup></p>\n<p>As a result of the damage in Tacloban and much of <a href="/wiki/Leyte" title="Leyte">Leyte</a>, thousands of people who once lived in the area left and made their way into less affected areas such as <a href="/wiki/Cebu_City" title="Cebu City">Cebu</a> and <a href="/wiki/Manila" title="Manila">Manila</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-123" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-123">[119]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Catbalogan" title="Catbalogan">Catbalogan</a> reported that their population more than doubled after the typhoon with the influx of refugees into the city.<sup id="cite_ref-124" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-124">[120]</a></sup> Around 20,000 people have fled to <a href="/wiki/Metro_Manila" title="Metro Manila">Manila</a> as a result of the storm.<sup id="cite_ref-125" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-125">[121]</a></sup></p>\n<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="International_response">International response</span><span C-17 Globemaster III for Humanitarian Aid and Relief (HADR) efforts.</td>\n<td style="text-align:center;"><sup id="cite_ref-BBC24906526_204-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBC24906526-204">[200]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-205" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-205">[201]</a></sup><br />\n<sup id="cite_ref-BBC24940632_206-0" class="reference"><a src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/a4/Flag_of_the_United_States.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_United_States.svg.png" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a></td>\n<td><span style="display:none" class="sortkey">7007867000000000000\xe2\x99\xa0</span>$86.7&#160;million</td>\n<td>Deployed the <a href="/wiki/USS_George_Washington_(CVN-73)" title="USS George Washington (CVN-73)">USS&#160;<i>George Washington</i>&#160;(CVN-73)</a> and her embarked <a href="/wiki/Carrier_Strike_Group_Five" class="mw-redirect" title="Carrier Strike Group Five">carrier strike group</a>, along with the <a href="/wiki/31st_Marine_Expeditionary_Unit" title="31st Marine Expeditionary Unit">31st Marine Expeditionary Unit</a>, embarked aboard the <a href="/wiki/USS_Ashland_(LSD_48)" class="mw-redirect" title="USS Ashland (LSD 48)">USS Ashland (LSD 48)</a> and <a href="/wiki/USS_Germantown_(LSD_42)" class="mw-redirect" title="USS Germantown (LSD 42)">USS Germantown (LSD 42)</a>, of Amphibious Squadron 11. At its peak, the U.S. military efforts included more than 13,400 military personnel from the <a href="/wiki/US_Marine_Corps" class="mw-redirect" title="US Marine Corps">US Marine Corps</a>, <a href="/wiki/US_Navy" class="mw-redirect" title="US Navy">US Navy</a> and <a href="/wiki/US_Air_Force" class="mw-redirect" title="US Air Force">US Air Force</a>. 66 aircraft were involved in the mission including the fixed-wing <a href="/wiki/C17_Globemaster" class="mw-redirect" title="C17 Globemaster">C17 Globemaster</a>, <a href="/wiki/C-130_Hercules" class="mw-redirect" title="C-130 Hercules">C-130 Hercules</a>, and <a href="/wiki/MV-22_Osprey" class="mw-redirect" title="MV-22 Osprey">MV-22 Osprey</a>, as well as <a href="/w/index.php?title=HH-60_helicopters&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="HH-60 helicopters (page does not exist)">HH-60 helicopters</a>. 12 U.S. Navy vessels responded in all. The US also deployed the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Agency_for_International_Development" title="United States Agency for International Development">United States Agency for International Development</a> and <a href="/wiki/Office_of_Foreign_Disaster_Assistance" title="Office of Foreign Disaster Assistance">Office of Foreign Disaster Assistance</a> crisis response teams to oversee military operations, and coordinate the US government response with the government of the Philippines.</td>\n<td></td>\n<td style="text-align:center;"><sup id="cite_ref-207" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-207">[203]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-usaid_haiyan_208-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-usaid_haiyan-208">[204]</a></sup><br />\n<sup id="cite_ref-209" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-209">[205]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-210" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-210">[206]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-211" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-213">[209]</a></sup></td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/21/Flag_of_Vietnam.svg/23px-Flag_of_Vietnam.svg.png" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" title="Vietnam">Vietnam</a></td>\n<td><span style="display:none" class="sortkey">7005100000000000000\xe2\x99\xa0</span>$100&#160;thousand</td>\n<td></td>\n<td></td>\n<td style="text-align:center;"><sup id="cite_ref-world-asia-24901993_214-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-world-asia-24901993-214">[210]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-215" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-215">[211]</a></sup></td>\n</tr>\n</table>\n<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Supranational_bodies">Supranational bodies</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Typhoon_Haiyan&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Supranational bodies">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>\n<div class="thumb tright">\n<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Tacloban_Typhoon_Haiyan_2013-11-14.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/77/Tacloban_Typhoon_Haiyan_2013-11-14.jpg/220px-Tacloban_Typhoon_Haiyan_2013-11-14.jpg" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/77/Tacloban_Typhoon_Haiyan_2013-11-14.jpg/330px-Tacloban_Typhoon_Haiyan_2013-11-14.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/77/Tacloban_Typhoon_Haiyan_2013-11-14.jpg/440px-Tacloban_Typhoon_Haiyan_2013-11-14.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4608" data-file-height="3072" /></a>\n<div class="thumbcaption">\n<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Tacloban_Typhoon_Haiyan_2013-11-14.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>\nDebris littering the streets of Tacloban City on November 14, nearly a week after the storm struck.</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n<div class="thumb tright">\n<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Basey_after_Yolanda2.JPG" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/ce/Basey_after_Yolanda2.JPG/220px-Basey_after_Yolanda2.JPG" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/ce/Basey_after_Yolanda2.JPG/330px-Basey_after_Yolanda2.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/ce/Basey_after_Yolanda2.JPG/440px-Basey_after_Yolanda2.JPG 2x" data-file-width="2592" data-file-height="1944" /></a>\n<div class="thumbcaption">\n<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Basey_after_Yolanda2.JPG" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>\nDevastation in the town of <a href="/wiki/Basey,_Samar" title="Basey, Samar">Basey</a>, <a href="/wiki/Samar" title="Samar">Samar</a>, where more than 300 individuals perished due to storm surge.</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n<p>The United Nations said it was going to increase critical relief operations as a result of the devastation caused by the typhoon. Its Manila office issued a statement that read, "Access remains a key challenge as some areas are still cut off from relief operations. Unknown numbers of survivors do not have basic necessities such as food, water and medicines and remain inaccessible for relief operations, as roads, airports and bridges were destroyed or covered in wreckage."<sup id="cite_ref-216" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-216">[212]</a></sup> The United Nations also began relief operations by this time; however, the severe damage to infrastructure hampered efforts to distribute supplies.<sup id="cite_ref-CBSNov10_106-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CBSNov10-106">[102]</a></sup> The UN activated the Cluster System, in which groups of humanitarian organizations (UN and non-UN) work to restore health, shelter, nutrition and economic activity.<sup id="cite_ref-217" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-217">[213]</a></sup></p>\n<p>The <a href="/wiki/World_Health_Organization" title="World Health Organization">World Health Organization</a>, which leads the Health Cluster, the largest one, has developed guidance on donations of medicine and healthcare equipment, so that the Philippines receives supplies appropriate for this emergency. According to <a href="/wiki/WHO" class="mw-redirect" title="WHO">WHO</a>, many people suffered cuts, wounds, and broken bones during the disaster and others were injured in flooding that followed the typhoon.<sup id="cite_ref-218" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-218">[214]</a></sup> Interpol announced that they would send in Interpol officers from Lyon to help local law enforcement identify any of the corpses that are unidentified.<sup id="cite_ref-219" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-219">[215]</a></sup></p>\n<p>The <a href="/wiki/World_Health_Organization" title="World Health Organization">World Health Organization</a> has spearheaded initiatives among help workers, especially from the <a href="/wiki/Department_of_Health_(Philippines)" title="Department of Health (Philippines)">Department of Health (Philippines)</a>, in extending Psychological First Aid to people in typhoon-affected areas. WHO Representative in the country Dr <a href="/wiki/Julie_Hall" title="Julie Hall">Julie Hall</a> foresees long-lasting effects from the typhoon. She calls for increased preparedness to give support to families and communities for the long-term, citing the need for more trained field workers.<sup id="cite_ref-220" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-220">[216]</a></sup></p>\n<h4><span id="Celebrities,_companies,_and_NGOs"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Celebrities.2C_companies.2C_and_NGOs">Celebrities, companies, and NGOs</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Typhoon_Haiyan&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Celebrities, companies, and NGOs">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>\n<p>American band <a href="/wiki/Journey_(band)" title="Journey (band)">Journey</a> donated $350,000 to help relief efforts in the Philippines, and its lead singer had a message for his homeland: "Don\'t Stop Believin\'". <a href="/wiki/Arnel_Pineda" title="Arnel Pineda">Arnel Pineda</a> (the band\'s Filipino vocalist) and the rest of the band announced the donation on November 15, 2013. It will go to the United Nations World Food Programme, which is providing Filipinos with food assistance. The donation should provide 1.4 million meals.<sup id="cite_ref-221" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-221">[217]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/IKEA" title="IKEA">IKEA</a>, <a href="/wiki/Walmart" title="Walmart">Walmart</a>, <a href="/wiki/Samsung" title="Samsung">Samsung</a>, and <a href="/wiki/HSBC" title="HSBC">HSBC</a> are among those taking advantage of the event to donate to those in need.<sup id="cite_ref-222" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-222">[218]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-223" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-223">[219]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Northwestern_Mutual" title="Northwestern Mutual">Northwestern Mutual</a> announced they will donate $100,000 to the <a href="/wiki/American_Red_Cross" title="American Red Cross">American Red Cross</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-prnewswire_224-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-prnewswire-224">[220]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/The_Coca-Cola_Company" title="The Coca-Cola Company">The Coca-Cola Company</a> says they have donated $2.5 million of their advertising budget to the relief efforts as of November 25.<sup id="cite_ref-huffpostnov35_225-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-huffpostnov35-225">[221]</a></sup> By mid-December <a href="/wiki/FIFA" title="FIFA">FIFA</a> donated $1 million.<sup id="cite_ref-226" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-226">[222]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/DHL" class="mw-redirect" title="DHL">DHL</a> deployed its Asia Pacific Disaster Response Team to the disaster areas to provide on-the-ground logistics support to assist with the relief effort in the aftermath of the devastating Typhoon Haiyan. Three rotating teams made up of volunteer employees from the Asia Pacific region were based at the Mactan Cebu Airport on Cebu island, providing support and assistance to the country\'s most affected areas west of Leyte Island, including Guiuan, Roxas, and Tacloban city.<sup id="cite_ref-227" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-227">[223]</a></sup> Many smaller initiatives were founded as well - e.g. to prepare by donating to children a typhoon-ready backpack as floating device.<sup id="cite_ref-228" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-228">[224]</a></sup></p>\n<div class="thumb tleft">\n<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:US_marines_Typhoon_Haiyan_relief.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/23/US_marines_Typhoon_Haiyan_relief.jpg/220px-US_marines_Typhoon_Haiyan_relief.jpg" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/23/US_marines_Typhoon_Haiyan_relief.jpg/330px-US_marines_Typhoon_Haiyan_relief.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/23/US_marines_Typhoon_Haiyan_relief.jpg/440px-US_marines_Typhoon_Haiyan_relief.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2048" data-file-height="1365" /></a>\n<div class="thumbcaption">\n<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:US_marines_Typhoon_Haiyan_relief.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>\n<a href="/wiki/U.S._Marines" class="mw-redirect" title="U.S. Marines">U.S. Marines</a> assisting in the Philippine disaster relief.</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n<p>Sixteen-time <a href="/wiki/NBA" class="mw-redirect" title="NBA">NBA</a> Champions <a href="/wiki/Los_Angeles_Lakers" title="Los Angeles Lakers">Los Angeles Lakers</a> donated $150,000 <sup id="cite_ref-229" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-229">[225]</a></sup> to the <a href="/wiki/Philippine_Red_Cross" title="Philippine Red Cross">Philippine Red Cross</a> to aid the typhoon affected victims. During their home game against the <a href="/wiki/Memphis_Grizzlies" title="Memphis Grizzlies">Memphis Grizzlies</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kobe_Bryant" title="Kobe Bryant">Kobe Bryant</a> handed the check to the Junior <a href="/wiki/NBA" class="mw-redirect" title="NBA">NBA</a> players representing the <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippines</a>. His teammate, <a href="/wiki/Pau_Gasol" title="Pau Gasol">Pau Gasol</a>, pledged to donate $1,000 per point to UNICEF<sup id="cite_ref-230" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-230">[226]</a></sup> with the directive to help victims of Super Typhoon Haiyan in the country as well. He scored 24 points in a won game against the <a href="/wiki/Golden_State_Warriors" title="Golden State Warriors">Golden State Warriors</a>. <a href="/wiki/Major_League_Baseball" title="Major League Baseball">Major League Baseball</a> donated $200,000 to <a href="/wiki/UNICEF" title="UNICEF">UNICEF</a> and the American Red Cross, with <a href="/wiki/Commissioner_of_Baseball" title="Commissioner of Baseball">Commissioner</a> <a href="/wiki/Bud_Selig" title="Bud Selig">Bud Selig</a> encouraging fans to donate to the organizations.<sup id="cite_ref-mlb_231-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-mlb-231">[227]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/UNICEF" title="UNICEF">UNICEF</a> delivered portable toilets and hygiene supplies to the region and also appealed for $34 million to help the four million children affected.<sup id="cite_ref-232" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-232">[228]</a></sup> The American Red Cross announced that they collected $11 million in donations for the Philippines Relief Fund.<sup id="cite_ref-233" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-233">[229]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Mercy_Corps" title="Mercy Corps">Mercy Corps</a> dispatched a "emergency response" team to help with humanitarian efforts.<sup id="cite_ref-theoregonian_234-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-theoregonian-234">[230]</a></sup> MAP International launched medical relief efforts providing over $10 million in medicines and supplies to the Philippines.</p>\n<p>Among the NGO responses, among the most comprehensive disaster response came from the Taiwan-based <cite class="citation web"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.tzuchi.org.ph/newsite/">"Buddhist Tzu Chi Foundation"</a>.</cite><span title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3ATyphoon+Haiyan&amp;rft.btitle=Buddhist+Tzu+Chi+Foundation&amp;rft.genre=unknown&amp;rft_id=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.tzuchi.org.ph%2Fnewsite%2F&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook" class="Z3988"><span style="display:none;">&#160;</span></span>, which organized a large-scale cash-for-work program in Tacloban from Nov 20 to Dec 8 with up to 31,000 participants per day, totaling nearly 300,000 day shifts. This operation not only helped clean out the thousands of tons of debris covering the city, but also kick-started the local economy. Tzu Chi also contributed emergency cash aid of 8000, 12000 or 15000 pesos depending on family size for over 60,000 families in the affected areas of Tacloban, Ormoc, Palo, Tanauan and Tunga, and has been providing free clinics, hot meals, and temporary class rooms for over 15 schools in the area. <a href="/wiki/Doctors_Without_Borders" class="mw-redirect" title="Doctors Without Borders">Doctors Without Borders</a> is sending 200 tons of aid.<sup id="cite_ref-world-asia-24901993_214-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-world-asia-24901993-214">[210]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-news24_235-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-news24-235">[231]</a></sup> The <a href="/wiki/International_Society_for_Krishna_Consciousness" title="International Society for Krishna Consciousness">International Society for Krishna Consciousness</a>\'s <a href="/wiki/Food_For_Life_Global" class="mw-redirect" title="Food For Life Global">Food For Life Global</a>, the world\'s largest vegan food relief organisation, raised money and provided vegan meals in the Philippines to Typhoon Haiyan survivors.<sup id="cite_ref-236" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-236">[232]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-237" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-237">[233]</a></sup> Other NGOs run by faith-based organisations that raised money and/or aided in the disaster relief efforts of Typhoon Haiyan included <a href="/wiki/Catholic_Relief_Services" title="Catholic Relief Services">Catholic Relief Services</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-CNNHaiyan_238-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CNNHaiyan-238">[234]</a></sup> Catholic Medical Mission Board (CMMB),<sup id="cite_ref-CNNHaiyan_238-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CNNHaiyan-238">[234]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Adventist_Development_and_Relief_Agency" title="Adventist Development and Relief Agency">Adventist Development and Relief Agency</a> (ADRA),<sup id="cite_ref-CNNHaiyan_238-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CNNHaiyan-238">[234]</a></sup> LDS Philanthropies,<sup id="cite_ref-239" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-239">[235]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/American_Jewish_Joint_Distribution_Committee" title="American Jewish Joint Distribution Committee">American Jewish Joint Distribution Committee</a> (AJJDC),<sup id="cite_ref-CNNHaiyan_238-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CNNHaiyan-238">[234]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Samaritan%27s_Purse" title="Samaritan\'s Purse">Samaritan\'s Purse</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-CNNHaiyan_238-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CNNHaiyan-238">[234]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Salvation_Army" class="mw-redirect" title="Salvation Army">Salvation Army</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-CNNHaiyan_238-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CNNHaiyan-238">[234]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Christian_Children%27s_Fund_of_Canada" title="Christian Children\'s Fund of Canada">Christian Children\'s Fund of Canada</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-CNNHaiyan_238-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CNNHaiyan-238">[234]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/MAP_International" title="MAP International">MAP International</a> and <a href="/wiki/World_Vision" class="mw-redirect" title="World Vision">World Vision</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-CNNHaiyan_238-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CNNHaiyan-238">[234]</a></sup></p>\n<p>The <a href="/wiki/Iglesia_Ni_Cristo" class="mw-redirect" title="Iglesia Ni Cristo">Iglesia Ni Cristo</a> (INC), the largest indigenous Christian church based in the Philippines held series of massive relief distributions and medical and dental missions to affected population of the storm to different parts of <a href="/wiki/Visayas" title="Visayas">Visayas</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-240" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-240">[236]</a></sup> The humanitarian mission was done under the <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.kabayankokapatidko.org/">"Lingap sa Mamamayan" (Aid for Humanity)</a> project in cooperation with the Felix Y. Manalo (FYM) Foundation Inc., the INC\xe2\x80\x99s charitable arm.<sup id="cite_ref-241" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-241">[237]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-242" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-242">[238]</a></sup> The church conducted the largest walk for a cause in the world (<a href="/wiki/Walkathon" title="Walkathon">walkathon</a>) on February 15, 2014, dubbed as \'Iglesia Ni Cristo World Wide Walk for Those Affected by Typhoon Yolanda/Haiyan\'.<sup id="cite_ref-243" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-243">[239]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-244" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-244">[240]</a></sup> The walk for a cause raised millions of money to help the victims of the super typhoon for the construction of their houses and shelters. The aim of the activity is to make the world understand that Haiyan survivors are still in dare need of help and financial assistance. Indeed, the worldwide walk caught the attention of the world when it breaks two <a href="/wiki/Guinness" title="Guinness">Guinness</a> world records as the largest charity walk in a single venue (<a href="/wiki/Manila,_Philippines" class="mw-redirect" title="Manila, Philippines">Manila, Philippines</a>) with 175,000 participants, and largest charity walk in 24 hours for multiple venues (from <a href="/wiki/Christchurch" title="Christchurch">Christchurch</a>, New Zealand to <a href="/wiki/Hawaii,_USA" class="mw-redirect" title="Hawaii, USA">Hawaii, USA</a>) in 13 time zones, 54 countries, 24 hours with 519, 521 participants.<sup id="cite_ref-245" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-245">[241]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-246" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-246">[242]</a></sup></p>\n<p>Celebrities such as <a href="/wiki/David_Beckham" title="David Beckham">David</a> and <a href="/wiki/Victoria_Beckham" title="Victoria Beckham">Victoria Beckham</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-247" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-247">[243]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Stephen_Colbert" title="Stephen Colbert">Stephen Colbert</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-248" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-248">[244]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Kim_Kardashian" title="Kim Kardashian">Kim Kardashian</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-249" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-249">[245]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/David_Guetta" title="David Guetta">David Guetta</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-250" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-250">[246]</a></sup> and <i><a href="/wiki/The_X_Factor_(TV_series)" class="mw-redirect" title="The X Factor (TV series)">The X Factor</a></i> contributed to the fundraising.<sup id="cite_ref-251" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-251">[247]</a></sup> On November 26, <a href="/wiki/ITunes" title="ITunes">iTunes</a> released a <a href="/wiki/Compilation_album" title="Compilation album">compilation album</a> entitled <i>Songs for the Philippines</i> featuring different artists, including <a href="/wiki/Katy_Perry" title="Katy Perry">Katy Perry</a>, <a href="/wiki/Madonna_(entertainer)" title="Madonna (entertainer)">Madonna</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bob_Dylan" title="Bob Dylan">Bob Dylan</a>, and <a href="/wiki/The_Beatles" title="The Beatles">The Beatles</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-usatodaynov25_252-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-usatodaynov25-252">[248]</a></sup> All proceeds will go to the <a href="/wiki/Philippine_Red_Cross" title="Philippine Red Cross">Philippine Red Cross</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-usatodaynov25_252-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-usatodaynov25-252">[248]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/OneRepublic" title="OneRepublic">OneRepublic</a> donated $100,000 on November 30, 2013.<sup id="cite_ref-253" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-253">[249]</a></sup> Other celebrities that offered their support included <a href="/wiki/Linkin_Park" title="Linkin Park">Linkin Park</a>, <a href="/wiki/The_Offspring" title="The Offspring">The Offspring</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-254" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-254">[250]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Alicia_Keys" title="Alicia Keys">Alicia Keys</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-255" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-255">[251]</a></sup> and Justin Bieber.<sup id="cite_ref-256" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-256">[252]</a></sup></p>\n<p>On the day of his death, actor <a href="/wiki/Paul_Walker" title="Paul Walker">Paul Walker</a> attended a charity event for his organization, Reach Out Worldwide, for the victims of the typhoon that was held right before his accident.<sup id="cite_ref-CNN1_257-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CNN1-257">[253]</a></sup></p>\n<p>On March 11, 2014, a benefit concert called <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.pinoyrelief.com/pinoyconcert">The Pinoy Relief Benefit Concert</a> was held at <a href="/wiki/Madison_Square_Garden" title="Madison Square Garden">Madison Square Garden</a> in New York, City. <a href="/wiki/Jennifer_Hudson" title="Jennifer Hudson">Jennifer Hudson</a>, <a href="/wiki/Pentatonix" title="Pentatonix">Pentatonix</a>, <a href="/wiki/A_Great_Big_World" title="A Great Big World">A Great Big World</a>, <a href="/wiki/Plain_White_T%27s" title="Plain White T\'s">Plain White T\'s</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jessica_Sanchez" title="Jessica Sanchez">Jessica Sanchez</a>, <a href="/wiki/Charice" class="mw-redirect" title="Charice">Charice</a> and REO Brothers performed. Special guests also included <a href="/wiki/Dr._Oz" class="mw-redirect" title="Dr. Oz">Dr. Oz</a>, <a href="/wiki/Dante_Basco" title="Dante Basco">Dante Basco</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bobby_Lopez" class="mw-redirect" title="Bobby Lopez">Bobby Lopez</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kristen_Anderson-Lopez" title="Kristen Anderson-Lopez">Kristen Anderson-Lopez</a> and <a href="/wiki/Apl.de.ap" title="Apl.de.ap">Apl.de.ap</a>. 100% of proceeds raised directly went to the Typhoon Haiyan survivors.<sup id="cite_ref-258" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-258">[254]</a></sup> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.pinoyrelief.com">Pinoy Relief</a> was created to help survivors and focus on three specific areas: restoring livelihoods, building classrooms and providing shelter in partnership with local NGOs, <a href="/wiki/Habitat_for_Humanity" title="Habitat for Humanity">Habitat for Humanity</a> Philippines and <a href="/wiki/Operation_Blessing" class="mw-redirect" title="Operation Blessing">Operation Blessing</a> Philippines.<sup id="cite_ref-259" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-259">[255]</a></sup></p>\n<p>On March 13, 2016, former <a href="/wiki/United_States_of_America" class="mw-redirect" title="United States of America">United States of America</a> vice president <a href="/wiki/Al_Gore" title="Al Gore">Al Gore</a>, visited Tacloban and delivered his speech in front of the survivors of Haiyan. He also dropped by at the MV Eva Jocelyn, a cargo ship that washed out inland during the typhoon and now converted into a memorial park.<sup id="cite_ref-260" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-260">[256]</a></sup></p>\n<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Politics_involving_aid_relief">Politics involving aid relief</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Typhoon_Haiyan&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Politics involving aid relief">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>\n<div class="thumb tright">\n<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:First_UK-funded_humanitarian_flight_arrives_in_Cebu,_Philippines_-_10826427444.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/97/First_UK-funded_humanitarian_flight_arrives_in_Cebu%2C_Philippines_-_10826427444.jpg/220px-First_UK-funded_humanitarian_flight_arrives_in_Cebu%2C_Philippines_-_10826427444.jpg" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/97/First_UK-funded_humanitarian_flight_arrives_in_Cebu%2C_Philippines_-_10826427444.jpg/330px-First_UK-funded_humanitarian_flight_arrives_in_Cebu%2C_Philippines_-_10826427444.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/97/First_UK-funded_humanitarian_flight_arrives_in_Cebu%2C_Philippines_-_10826427444.jpg/440px-First_UK-funded_humanitarian_flight_arrives_in_Cebu%2C_Philippines_-_10826427444.jpg 2x" data-file-width="5616" data-file-height="3744" /></a>\n<div class="thumbcaption">\n<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:First_UK-funded_humanitarian_flight_arrives_in_Cebu,_Philippines_-_10826427444.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>\nFirst UK-funded humanitarian flight arrives at <a href="/wiki/Mactan-Cebu_International_Airport" class="mw-redirect" title="Mactan-Cebu International Airport">Mactan-Cebu International Airport</a>.</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n<div class="thumb tright">\n<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Philippine_island_of_Binuluanguan_Following_Typhoon_Haiyan_MOD_45156472.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/10/Philippine_island_of_Binuluanguan_Following_Typhoon_Haiyan_MOD_45156472.jpg/220px-Philippine_island_of_Binuluanguan_Following_Typhoon_Haiyan_MOD_45156472.jpg" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/10/Philippine_island_of_Binuluanguan_Following_Typhoon_Haiyan_MOD_45156472.jpg/330px-Philippine_island_of_Binuluanguan_Following_Typhoon_Haiyan_MOD_45156472.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/10/Philippine_island_of_Binuluanguan_Following_Typhoon_Haiyan_MOD_45156472.jpg/440px-Philippine_island_of_Binuluanguan_Following_Typhoon_Haiyan_MOD_45156472.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3600" data-file-height="2400" /></a>\n<div class="thumbcaption">\n<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Philippine_island_of_Binuluanguan_Following_Typhoon_Haiyan_MOD_45156472.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>\nThe island of Binuluanguan overflown by a helicopter from HMS <i>Daring</i>.</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n<p>The aid contributions of China and the United States were given focus with regards to their involvement in the politics of the <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippines</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-261" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-261">[257]</a></sup> Apart from having the two largest economies in the world, both countries are involved in a complex relationship with the island country. China is currently <a href="/wiki/Spratly_islands_dispute" class="mw-redirect" title="Spratly islands dispute">disputing</a> the <a href="/wiki/Spratly_Islands" title="Spratly Islands">Spratly Islands</a> in the <a href="/wiki/South_China_Sea" title="South China Sea">South China Sea</a> with the Philippines while the United States used to be an occupying power and currently has a <a href="/wiki/Mutual_Defense_Treaty_(U.S.%E2%80%93Philippines)" class="mw-redirect" title="Mutual Defense Treaty (U.S.\xe2\x80\x93Philippines)">mutual defense treaty with the islands</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-262" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-262">[258]</a></sup></p>\n<p>China was initially criticized for its meager contribution of US $100,000 cash each from the government and the Chinese Red Cross to the typhoon victims, which led to commentary about its disputes with the Philippines.<sup id="cite_ref-263" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-263">[259]</a></sup> Earlier in 2013, <a href="/wiki/Philippines_v._China" title="Philippines v. China">the Philippines sued China</a> over the <a href="/wiki/Nine-dotted_line" class="mw-redirect" title="Nine-dotted line">nine-dotted line</a>. Commentators attribute this low amount to China\'s intentions to isolate the Philippines while strengthening its ties with the rest of Southeast Asia.<sup id="cite_ref-264" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-264">[260]</a></sup> The move had mixed reactions from the public of China with some commending its decision while others, such as <i><a href="/wiki/The_Global_Times" class="mw-redirect" title="The Global Times">The Global Times</a></i>, insisted that China should be a responsible power. China later increased its contributions by US$1.64 million in supplies <sup id="cite_ref-China_Increases_Aid_to_Philippines_140-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-China_Increases_Aid_to_Philippines-140">[136]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-265" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-265">[261]</a></sup> and sent its naval hospital ship <i><a href="/wiki/Peace_Ark" class="mw-redirect" title="Peace Ark">Peace Ark</a></i> for disaster relief."<sup id="cite_ref-peace-ark_141-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-peace-ark-141">[137]</a></sup></p>\n<p>The contributions of the United States was in contrast to that of China. It gave the Philippines an amount of US$51.9 million worth of aid apart and deployed the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Marines" class="mw-redirect" title="United States Marines">United States Marines</a>, <a href="/wiki/United_States_Navy" title="United States Navy">United States Navy</a> and <a href="/wiki/United_States_Air_Force" title="United States Air Force">United States Air Force</a> in order to assist with the humanitarian operations.<sup id="cite_ref-266" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-266">[262]</a></sup> This was seen by observers as part of the Asia pivot that the United States government had previously announced.<sup id="cite_ref-267" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-267">[263]</a></sup> The Philippine government had been discussing with the U.S. plans regarding the deployment of U.S. military troops within the country. Aid contributions of the U.S. was seen as a sign of goodwill in order to further strengthen relations.<sup id="cite_ref-268" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-268">[264]</a></sup></p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Vietnam_3">Vietnam</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Typhoon_Haiyan&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Vietnam">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>Following Typhoon Haiyan\'s landfall in Vietnam, widespread search and rescue missions took place in the affected provinces. Damage assessments were also conducted in 13 provinces to determine what aid was needed. The IFRC began distribution of relief supplies and assisted residents in returning home by November 12. Operations regarding the aftermath of Typhoon Wutip were temporarily suspended due to Haiyan.<sup id="cite_ref-VietnamRW2_51-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-VietnamRW2-51">[48]</a></sup></p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Climate_change">Climate change</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Typhoon_Haiyan&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Climate change">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>Political leaders and climate scientists <a href="/wiki/Effects_of_global_warming" title="Effects of global warming">connected</a> the typhoon to <a href="/wiki/Global_warming" title="Global warming">climate change</a>, both at the time and subsequently<sup id="cite_ref-269" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-269">[265]</a></sup> and led to calls for climate justice.<sup id="cite_ref-270" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-270">[266]</a></sup> The <a href="/wiki/2013_United_Nations_Climate_Change_Conference" title="2013 United Nations Climate Change Conference">2013 United Nations Climate Change Conference</a> was coincidentally in progress when the typhoon struck and Yeb Sa\xc3\xb1o, the lead negotiator of the <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippines</a> delegation, received a standing ovation at the conference when he declared a hunger strike.</p>\n<blockquote class="templatequote">\n<p>In solidarity with my countrymen who are struggling to find food back home, I will now commence a voluntary fasting for the climate; this means I will voluntarily refrain from eating food during this <a href="/wiki/2013_United_Nations_Climate_Change_Conference" title="2013 United Nations Climate Change Conference">COP</a>, until a meaningful outcome is in sight.</p>\n<div class="templatequotecite">\xe2\x80\x94\xe2\x80\x89<cite>Yeb Sa\xc3\xb1o<sup id="cite_ref-271" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-271">[267]</a></sup></cite></div>\n</blockquote>\n<p>Several delegates, including American delegate Collin Reese, joined him in fasting. Sixty people from <a href="/wiki/Climate_Action_Network" title="Climate Action Network">Climate Action Network</a>, an <a href="/wiki/Umbrella_group" class="mw-redirect" title="Umbrella group">umbrella group</a> of environmental non-governmental organisations, also joined the hunger strike.<sup id="cite_ref-272" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-272">[268]</a></sup></p>\n<p>The correlation between the increasing intensity of storms and the progression of climate change was discussed by climate scientists. "Typhoons, hurricanes and all tropical storms draw their vast energy from the warmth of the sea. We know sea-surface temperatures are warming pretty much around the planet, so that\'s a pretty direct influence of climate change on the nature of the storm," said <a href="/wiki/Will_Steffen" title="Will Steffen">Will Steffen</a>, director of the <a href="/wiki/Australian_National_University" title="Australian National University">Australian National University</a> climate change institute.<sup id="cite_ref-Guardian-13-11-12_273-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Guardian-13-11-12-273">[269]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Myles_Allen" title="Myles Allen">Myles Allen</a>, head of the climate dynamics group at the <a href="/wiki/University_of_Oxford" title="University of Oxford">University of Oxford</a>, said that "The current consensus is that climate change is not making the risk of hurricanes any greater, but there are physical arguments and evidence that there is a risk of more intense hurricanes."<sup id="cite_ref-Guardian-13-11-12_273-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Guardian-13-11-12-273">[269]</a></sup> <i>The Huffington Post</i> made the point that the 70% <a href="/wiki/Deforestation_in_the_Philippines" title="Deforestation in the Philippines">deforestation of the Philippines</a> since 1900, as reported by the national <a href="/wiki/Department_of_Environment_and_Natural_Resources_(Philippines)" title="Department of Environment and Natural Resources (Philippines)">Forest Management Bureau</a>, made far more lethal flooding from cyclones like Haiyan more likely.<sup id="cite_ref-274" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-274">[270]</a></sup> The <a href="/wiki/IPCC_Fifth_Assessment_Report" title="IPCC Fifth Assessment Report">IPCC Fifth Assessment Report</a> had stated in September of the same year that "Time series of cyclone indices such as power dissipation, an aggregate compound of tropical cyclone frequency, duration, and intensity that measures total wind energy by tropical cyclones, show upward trends in the North Atlantic and weaker upward trends in the western North Pacific since the late 1970s."<sup id="cite_ref-Guardian-13-11-12_273-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Guardian-13-11-12-273">[269]</a></sup></p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="In_popular_media">In popular media</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Typhoon_Haiyan&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: In popular media">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<p>A detailed analysis of Typhoon Haiyan and its destruction in the Philippines was featured in a documentary called <i>Megastorm: World\'s Biggest Typhoon</i>. It aired on December 30, 2013 on <a href="/wiki/Discovery_Channel" title="Discovery Channel">Discovery Channel</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-275" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-275">[271]</a></sup></p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="See_also">See also</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Typhoon_Haiyan&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: See also">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<div role="navigation" neighboring islands of Bohol and Cebu less than a month before Haiyan struck</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Typhoons_in_the_Philippines" title="Typhoons in the Philippines">Typhoons in the Haiyan</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Tropical_Storm_Thelma" title="Tropical Storm Thelma">Tropical Storm Thelma (Uring; 1991)</a> \xe2\x80\x93 second deadliest Philippine tropical cyclone<sup title="Typhoon Son-Tinh">Typhoon Son-Tinh (Ofel, 2012)</a> \xe2\x80\x93 hit the same area a year ago and had a similar track with Haiyan</li>\n</ul>\n</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/List_of_most_intense_tropical_cyclones" class="mw-redirect" title="List of most intense tropical cyclones">Other most intense tropical cyclones</a>\n<ul>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Typhoon_Tip" title="Typhoon Tip">Typhoon Tip (Warling, 1979)</a> \xe2\x80\x93 strongest tropical cyclone based on pressure in recorded history</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Typhoon_Rita_(1978)" title="Typhoon Rita (1978)">Typhoon Rita (Kading, 1978)</a></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Patricia" title="Hurricane Patricia">Hurricane Patricia</a> \xe2\x80\x93 strongest tropical cyclone based on reliably measured maximum sustained winds in recorded history.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Typhoon_Nancy" class="mw-redirect" title="Typhoon Nancy">Typhoon Nancy</a></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Typhoon_Nora_(1973)" title="Typhoon Nora (1973)">Typhoon Nora (Luming, 1973)</a></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Typhoon_Gay_(1992)" title="Typhoon Gay (1992)">Typhoon Gay (1992)</a></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Typhoon_Meranti" title="Typhoon Meranti">Typhoon Meranti</a></li>\n</ul>\n</li>\n</ul>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Notes">Notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Typhoon_Haiyan&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Notes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<div class="reflist" style="list-style-type: decimal;">\n<div class="mw-references-wrap">\n<ol class="references">\n<li id="cite_note-9"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-9">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">The <a href="/wiki/Joint_Typhoon_Warning_Center" title="Joint Typhoon Warning Center">Joint Typhoon Warning Center</a> is a joint <a href="/wiki/United_States_Navy" title="United States Navy">United States Navy</a> \xe2\x80\x93 <a href="/wiki/United_States_Air_Force" title="United States Air Force">United States Air Force</a> task force that issues tropical cyclone warnings for the western Pacific Ocean and other regions.<sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">[8]</a></sup></span></li>\n<li id="cite_note-13"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-13">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">The <a href="/wiki/Japan_Meteorological_Agency" title="Japan Meteorological Agency">Japan Meteorological Agency</a> (JMA) is the official <a href="/wiki/Regional_Specialized_Meteorological_Center" title="Regional Specialized Meteorological Center">Regional Specialized Meteorological Center</a> for the western Pacific Ocean.<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">[11]</a></sup></span></li>\n<li id="cite_note-STY-17"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-STY_17-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">A super typhoon is defined as a tropical cyclone with one-minute sustained winds of at least 240 km/h (150 mph).<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">[14]</a></sup></span></li>\n<li id="cite_note-damage-55"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-damage_55-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><b>Total damages</b> figure includes agriculture, infrastructure, casualties, etc. damages.</span></li>\n</ol>\n</div>\n</div>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="References">References</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Typhoon_Haiyan&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit
